## üìÅ Project Structure

```sh
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ cross-sums-clone.git/
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ README.md
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ backend
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .env
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ __pycache__
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ app
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ app.db
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ main.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ requirements.txt
    ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ venv
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ package-lock.json
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ package.json
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ public
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ favicon.ico
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ index.html
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ logo192.png
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ logo512.png
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ manifest.json
    ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ robots.txt
    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ src
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ App.css
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ App.js
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ App.test.js
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Board.css
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Board.js
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ components
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ index.css
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ index.js
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ logo.svg
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ pages
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ reportWebVitals.js
        ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ setupTests.js
```

## üöÄ Getting Started

### ‚òëÔ∏è Prerequisites

Before getting started with cross-sums-clone.git, ensure your runtime environment meets the following requirements:

- **Programming Language:** Python
- **Package Manager:** Npm, Pip
- **Container Runtime:** Docker


### ‚öôÔ∏è Installation

Install cross-sums-clone.git using one of the following methods:

**Build from source:**

1. Clone the cross-sums-clone.git repository:
```sh
‚ùØ git clone https://github.com/rishixkumar/cross-sums-clone.git
```

2. Navigate to the project directory:
```sh
‚ùØ cd cross-sums-clone.git
```

3. Install the project dependencies:


**Using `npm`** &nbsp; [<img align="center" src="" />]()

```sh
‚ùØ echo 'INSERT-INSTALL-COMMAND-HERE'
```


**Using `pip`** &nbsp; [<img align="center" src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Pip-3776AB.svg?style={badge_style}&logo=pypi&logoColor=white" />](https://pypi.org/project/pip/)

```sh
‚ùØ pip install -r backend/requirements.txt
```


**Using `docker`** &nbsp; [<img align="center" src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Docker-2CA5E0.svg?style={badge_style}&logo=docker&logoColor=white" />](https://www.docker.com/)

```sh
‚ùØ docker build -t rishixkumar/cross-sums-clone.git .
```




### ü§ñ Usage
Run cross-sums-clone.git using the following command:
**Using `npm`** &nbsp; [<img align="center" src="" />]()

```sh
‚ùØ echo 'INSERT-RUN-COMMAND-HERE'
```


**Using `pip`** &nbsp; [<img align="center" src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Pip-3776AB.svg?style={badge_style}&logo=pypi&logoColor=white" />](https://pypi.org/project/pip/)

```sh
‚ùØ python {entrypoint}
```


**Using `docker`** &nbsp; [<img align="center" src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Docker-2CA5E0.svg?style={badge_style}&logo=docker&logoColor=white" />](https://www.docker.com/)

```sh
‚ùØ docker run -it {image_name}
```


### üß™ Testing
Run the test suite using the following command:
**Using `npm`** &nbsp; [<img align="center" src="" />]()

```sh
‚ùØ echo 'INSERT-TEST-COMMAND-HERE'
```


**Using `pip`** &nbsp; [<img align="center" src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Pip-3776AB.svg?style={badge_style}&logo=pypi&logoColor=white" />](https://pypi.org/project/pip/)

```sh
‚ùØ pytest
```

## üî∞ Contributing

- **üí¨ [Join the Discussions](https://github.com/rishixkumar/cross-sums-clone.git/discussions)**: Share your insights, provide feedback, or ask questions.
- **üêõ [Report Issues](https://github.com/rishixkumar/cross-sums-clone.git/issues)**: Submit bugs found or log feature requests for the `cross-sums-clone.git` project.
- **üí° [Submit Pull Requests](https://github.com/rishixkumar/cross-sums-clone.git/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md)**: Review open PRs, and submit your own PRs.

<details closed>
<summary>Contributing Guidelines</summary>

1. **Fork the Repository**: Start by forking the project repository to your github account.
2. **Clone Locally**: Clone the forked repository to your local machine using a git client.
   ```sh
   git clone https://github.com/rishixkumar/cross-sums-clone.git
   ```
3. **Create a New Branch**: Always work on a new branch, giving it a descriptive name.
   ```sh
   git checkout -b new-feature-x
   ```
4. **Make Your Changes**: Develop and test your changes locally.
5. **Commit Your Changes**: Commit with a clear message describing your updates.
   ```sh
   git commit -m 'Implemented new feature x.'
   ```
6. **Push to github**: Push the changes to your forked repository.
   ```sh
   git push origin new-feature-x
   ```
7. **Submit a Pull Request**: Create a PR against the original project repository. Clearly describe the changes and their motivations.
8. **Review**: Once your PR is reviewed and approved, it will be merged into the main branch. Congratulations on your contribution!
</details>

<details closed>
<summary>Contributor Graph</summary>
<br>
<p align="left">
   <a href="https://github.com{/rishixkumar/cross-sums-clone.git/}graphs/contributors">
      <img src="https://contrib.rocks/image?repo=rishixkumar/cross-sums-clone.git">
   </a>
</p>
</details>
